 Myth - 1
 garbhvatee mahila ke saamne sundar se bachche kii tasviir lagane se hone vaala baccha bhi khubasurat paidaa hota he
 Reality - Actually, there is nothing like that

 myth-2

 vaastaviktaa-ye baat saraasar galat he

 Myth-3
 subah kaa pehla niwala safed khaanaa chahie
 This gives the child a fair complexion
 vaastaviktaa-ye bhi apane aap main ek bahut hi bada myth he

 myth-4
 During eclipse the pregnant woman should hide and avoid any kind of activity
 vaastaviktaa-garbhavastha ke dauraan mahilaon ko grahan ke dauraan kamare main chupchaap baith jane kii salaah di jaati he
 But the point to think is that eclipse is a definite process and it has no effect on the child's birth
 haalanki, iskaa matlab ye bilkul nahin he ki grahan ko beparwaah hokar nangi ankhon se dekha jaae lekin, ye baat keval garbhvatee mahilaon ke liye nahin balki sabhi ke liye lagu hoti he
 Myth-5
 garbh ke aakaar se bachche kaa ling pataa chal jaataa he
 Reality - This is also a very interesting myth in itself
 garbh kaa aakaar, garbh main bachche kii pojishan ke bare main bataata he
 The size of the womb has no connection with the sex of the baby
 myth-6
 The gender of the mother reveals the sex of the child
